(**********************************************************************************

 The double category of lenses

 In this file, we define the double category of lenses. Suppose that `C` is a
 category with binary products. Then we define the following double category:
 - Objects: those of `C`
 - Vertical morphisms: morphisms in `C`
 - Horizontal morphisms: lenses in `C`
 The squares in this double category are commutative squares.

 This double category is essentially also constructed in Proposition 2.0.4 in
 "Categories of Optics" by Riley ( https://arxiv.org/pdf/1809.00738.pdf).
 There are two difference between the formalization in this file and the reference.
 In the reference, a category of lenses is constructed, and this amounts to
 constructing the horizontal composition and identities of lenses, whereas here
 a double category is constructed. The other difference is the method taken: the
 reference uses an abstract theorem about optics, whereas we construct the desired
 double category directly.

 Note that a double category of lenses has also been considered by Clarke in
 "The double category of lenses" (https://figshare.mq.edu.au/articles/thesis/The_double_category_of_lenses/22045073/1).
 The difference between the formalization and that thesis is that a different
 notion of lens is considered. Clarke looks at delta-lenses, so the resulting
 double category is as follows:
 - Objects: categories
 - Vertical morphisms: delta-lenses
 - Horizontal morphisms: functors
 This is different from what we look at, because we look at lenses in a category
 with finite products.

 We provide both a univalent and a strict version.

 Contents
 1. The horizontal identity
 2. Horizontal composition
 3. Unitors and associators
 4. The double category
 5. The strict double category

 **********************************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.

Section LensesDoubleCat.
  Context (C : category)
          (PC : BinProducts C).

  (** * 1. The horizontal identity *)
  
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)

  
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)

    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ x : C, twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x x
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), ?I x -->[ f ][ f] ?I y

    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ x : C, twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x x
 exact (identity_lens _ _).
    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
identity_lens C PC x -->[ f ][ f] identity_lens C PC y
 exact (λ x y f, identity_lens_mor _ _ f).
  Defined.

  
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)

  
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)

    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id_laws ?I

    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)
 exact lenses_double_cat_hor_id_data.
    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_id_laws lenses_double_cat_hor_id_data
 abstract
        (split ;
         intros ;
         apply discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat).
  Defined.

  (** * 2. Horizontal composition *)
  
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_comp_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)

  
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
hor_comp_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC)

    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ x y z : C,
twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
→ twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z
  → twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x z
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ (x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁ z₂ : C) (v₁ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(v₂ : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧) (v₃ : C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧)
(h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x₁ y₁)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y₁ z₁)
(k₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x₂ y₂)
(k₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y₂ z₂),
h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
→ h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
  → ?Cm x₁ y₁ z₁ h₁ h₂ -->[ v₁
    ][ v₃] ?Cm x₂ y₂ z₂ k₁ k₂

    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ x y z : C,
twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
→ twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z
  → twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x z
 exact (λ x y z l₁ l₂, comp_lens _ _ l₁ l₂).
    
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
∏ (x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁ z₂ : C) (v₁ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(v₂ : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧) (v₃ : C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧)
(h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x₁ y₁)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y₁ z₁)
(k₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x₂ y₂)
(k₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y₂ z₂),
h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
→ h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
  → (λ (x y z : C)
     (l₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y)
     (l₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z),
     comp_lens C PC l₁ l₂) x₁ y₁ z₁ h₁ h₂ -->[ v₁
    ][ v₃] (λ (x y z : C)
            (l₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y)
            (l₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z),
            comp_lens C PC l₁ l₂) x₂ y₂ z₂ k₁ k₂
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ φ ψ, comp_lens_mor _ _ φ ψ).
  Defined.

         intros ;
         apply discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat).
  Defined.

PC: BinProducts C
double_lunitor_data lenses_double_cat_hor_id
  lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
 
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y)
  (double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
     (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id x) f) f

      
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
  (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id x) f -->[
identity_z_iso x ][ identity_z_iso y] f
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
is_iso_twosided_disp (pr2 (identity_z_iso x))
  (pr2 (identity_z_iso y)) ?fg

      
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
  (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id x) f -->[
identity_z_iso x ][ identity_z_iso y] f
 
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
id₁ x · lens_get C PC f · id₁ y =
id₁ x · lens_get C PC f
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x) (PC (PC y x) x)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
       (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
· BinProductPr1 C (PC x x) · id₁ x =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

        
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
id₁ x · lens_get C PC f · id₁ y =
id₁ x · lens_get C PC f
 
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
lens_get C PC f = lens_get C PC f

          apply idpath.
        
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x) (PC (PC y x) x)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
       (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
· BinProductPr1 C (PC x x) · id₁ x =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f
 
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x) (PC (PC y x) x)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
       (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
· BinProductPr1 C (PC x x) =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x) (PC (PC y x) x)
     (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
   · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x)) =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· (BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
   · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)) =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
    (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
id₁ (PC y x)
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
    (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          apply idpath.
      
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
is_iso_twosided_disp (pr2 (identity_z_iso x))
  (pr2 (identity_z_iso y))
  (make_lens_mor C PC
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
        (id₁ x · lens_get C PC f) (lens_get C PC f)
        (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧, p · id₁ y = p)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
           (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
           (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧, p = lens_get C PC f)
           (idpath (lens_get C PC f))
           (id_right (lens_get C PC f)))
        (id_left (lens_get C PC f))
      :
      lens_get C PC
        (double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
           (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id x) f)
      · identity_z_iso y =
      identity_z_iso x · lens_get C PC f)
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
           (id₁ (PC y x)) (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
             (PC (PC y x) x)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
                (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
             (id₁ x) · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x)
         · id₁ x)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
           (id₁ (PC y x)) (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
             (PC (PC y x) x)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
                (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
             (id₁ x) · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x))
        (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
         p =
         BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
              (id₁ (PC y x))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
                (PC (PC y x) x)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                   (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                 · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
            · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x))
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
              (id₁ (PC y x))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
            · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                  · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x)))
           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
            p =
            BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
           (internal_paths_rew_r
              (C ⟦ PC (PC y x) x, x ⟧)
              (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                  · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x))
              (BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
               · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                  · lens_put C PC f))
              (λ p : C ⟦ PC (PC y x) x, x ⟧,
               BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (id₁ (PC y x))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)) · p =
               BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
                 (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
              (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                    (id₁ (PC y x))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                  · (BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                        · lens_put C PC f)))
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                    (id₁ (PC y x))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
                  · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                       (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                     · lens_put C PC f))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
                  p =
                  BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                  · lens_put C PC f)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                       (id₁ (PC y x))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                        · lens_put C PC f))
                    (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                       (id₁ (PC y x))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x)
                     · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                         (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                     · lens_put C PC f)
                    (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
                     p =
                     BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                       (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                     · lens_put C PC f)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧)
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y x) x)
                          (id₁ (PC y x))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                        · BinProductPr1 C
                            (PC (PC y x) x))
                       (id₁ (PC y x))
                       (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧,
                        p
                        · BinProductOfArrows C
                            (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                            (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f =
                        BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                        · lens_put C PC f)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧)
                          (id₁ (PC y x)
                           · BinProductOfArrows C
                               (PC y x) (PC y x)
                               (id₁ y) (id₁ x))
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                             (id₁ x))
                          (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧,
                           p · lens_put C PC f =
                           BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                             (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
                          (idpath
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y x) (PC y x)
                                (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                              · lens_put C PC f))
                          (id_left
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y x) (PC y x)
                                (id₁ y) (id₁ x))))
                       (BinProductPr1Commutes C
                          (PC y x) x (PC (PC y x) x)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ (PC y x))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))))
                    (assoc
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y x) x)
                          (id₁ (PC y x))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                        · BinProductPr1 C
                            (PC (PC y x) x))
                       (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x))
                       (lens_put C PC f)))
                 (assoc
                    (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                       (id₁ (PC y x))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)))
                    (BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y x) x))
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                       (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                     · lens_put C PC f)))
              (BinProductOfArrowsPr1 C (PC x x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                  · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)))
           (assoc'
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (id₁ (PC y x))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)))
              (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                  · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x))
              (BinProductPr1 C (PC x x))))
        (id_right
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
              (id₁ (PC y x))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x x)
                (PC (PC y x) x)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                   (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
                 · lens_put C PC f) (id₁ x)
            · BinProductPr1 C (PC x x)))
      :
      lens_put C PC
        (double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
           (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id x) f)
      · identity_z_iso x =
      BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
        (identity_z_iso y) (identity_z_iso x)
      · lens_put C PC f))
 apply discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat.

C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x₂ y₂
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
τ: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
trb₂ (make_iso_twosided_disp
        (make_lens_mor C PC
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
              (id₁ x₁ · lens_get C PC h₁)
              (lens_get C PC h₁)
              (λ p : C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧, p · id₁ y₁ = p)
              (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
                 (lens_get C PC h₁ · id₁ y₁)
                 (lens_get C PC h₁)
                 (λ p : C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧,
                  p = lens_get C PC h₁)
                 (idpath (lens_get C PC h₁))
                 (id_right (lens_get C PC h₁)))
              (id_left (lens_get C PC h₁)))
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                 (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
               · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₁ x₁)
                   (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                      (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                    · lens_put C PC h₁) (id₁ x₁)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₁ x₁) · id₁ x₁)
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                 (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
               · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₁ x₁)
                   (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                      (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                    · lens_put C PC h₁) (id₁ x₁)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₁ x₁))
              (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧,
               p =
               BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                 (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
               · lens_put C PC h₁)
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                    (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                  · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₁ x₁)
                      (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                      (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                         (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                       · lens_put C PC h₁) (id₁ x₁)
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₁ x₁))
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                    (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                  · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₁ x₁)
                       (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₁ x₁) (PC y₁ x₁)
                          (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                        · lens_put C PC h₁) (id₁ x₁)
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₁ x₁)))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧,
                  p =
                  BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                    (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                  · lens_put C PC h₁)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁, x₁ ⟧)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₁ x₁)
                       (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₁ x₁) (PC y₁ x₁)
                          (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                        · lens_put C PC h₁) (id₁ x₁)
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₁ x₁))
                    (BinProductPr1 C
                       (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₁ x₁) (PC y₁ x₁)
                          (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                        · lens_put C PC h₁))
                    (λ p : C ⟦ PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁, x₁ ⟧,
                     BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                       (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                     · p =
                     BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                       (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                     · lens_put C PC h₁)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                          (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                        · (BinProductPr1 C
                             (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                           · (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y₁ x₁) (PC y₁ x₁)
                                (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                              · lens_put C PC h₁)))
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                          (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))

                            (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                        · (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₁ x₁) (PC y₁ x₁)

                           · lens_put C PC h₁))
                       (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧,
                        p =
                        BinProductOfArrows C

                        · lens_put C PC h₁)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)

                                 p · lens_put C PC h₁ =

        (let X :=

                                    ... · ...)

                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₁ x₁)))))) ;;2 τ) =

make_iso_twosided_disp
  (make_lens_mor C PC
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
        (id₁ x₂ · lens_get C PC h₂) (lens_get C PC h₂)
        (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧, p · id₁ y₂ = p)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
           (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)
           (lens_get C PC h₂)
           (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧, p = lens_get C PC h₂)
           (idpath (lens_get C PC h₂))
           (id_right (lens_get C PC h₂)))
        (id_left (lens_get C PC h₂)))
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
           (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
           (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
              · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
         · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂) · id₁ x₂)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
           (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
           (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
              · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
         · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))
        (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
         p =
         BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
           (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                   (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                 · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
            · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                 (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂)))
           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
            p =
            BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
              (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
           (internal_paths_rew_r
              (C ⟦ PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂, x₂ ⟧)
              (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                 (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
               · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂))
              (λ p : C ⟦ PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂, x₂ ⟧,
               BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)) · p =
               BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                 (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · lens_put C PC h₂)
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                  · (BinProductPr1 C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂)))
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                  · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                  p =
                  BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                     · BinProductPr1 C
                         (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂))
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                     · BinProductPr1 C
                         (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                     · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                         (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂)
                    (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                     p =
                     BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                        · BinProductPr1 C
                            (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂))
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧,
                        p
                        · BinProductOfArrows C
                            (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                            (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂ =
                        BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂)
                           · BinProductOfArrows C
                               (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                               (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))
                          (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂,
                                 PC y₂ x₂ ⟧,
                           p · lens_put C PC h₂ =
                           BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                           · lens_put C PC h₂)
                          (idpath
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                                (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                              · lens_put C PC h₂))
                          (id_left
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                                (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))))
                       (BinProductPr1Commutes C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) x₂
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))))
                    (assoc
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                        · BinProductPr1 C
                            (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂))
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))
                       (lens_put C PC h₂)))
                 (assoc
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)))
                    (BinProductPr1 C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂))
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂)))
              (BinProductOfArrowsPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂)
                 (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)))
           (assoc'
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)))
              (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                 (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂))
              (BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))))
        (id_right
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                   (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                 · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
            · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂)))))
  (let X :=
     λ (C : category) (prodC : BinProducts C),
     pr2 (discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat C prodC)
     in
   let X0 :=
     λ (C : category) (prodC : BinProducts C),
     pr1 (X C prodC) in
   X0 C PC x₂ x₂ y₂ y₂
     (double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp
        (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id x₂) h₂) h₂
     (pr1 (identity_z_iso x₂))
     (pr1 (identity_z_iso y₂))
     (pr2 (identity_z_iso x₂))
     (pr2 (identity_z_iso y₂))
     (make_lens_mor C PC
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
           (id₁ x₂ · lens_get C PC h₂)
           (lens_get C PC h₂)
           (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧, p · id₁ y₂ = p)
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
              (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)
              (lens_get C PC h₂)
              (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧,
               p = lens_get C PC h₂)
              (idpath (lens_get C PC h₂))
              (id_right (lens_get C PC h₂)))
           (id_left (lens_get C PC h₂)))
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                   (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                 · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
            · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂) · id₁ x₂)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                   (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                 · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
            · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))
           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
            p =
            BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
              (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
               · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                   (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                      (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                    · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
               · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                    (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂)))
              (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
               p =
               BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                 (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · lens_put C PC h₂)
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (C ⟦ PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                    (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr1 C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                  · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                  BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)) · p =
                  BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                  · lens_put C PC h₂)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                     · (BinProductPr1 C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                        · (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                           · lens_put C PC h₂)))
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                     · BinProductPr1 C
                         (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂))
                    (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                     p =
                     BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                        · BinProductPr1 C
                            (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                        · (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                           · lens_put C PC h₂))
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                        · BinProductPr1 C
                            (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                        · BinProductOfArrows C
                            (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                            (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                        p =
                        BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                          (BinProductArrow C
                             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                             (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                             (BinProductPr2 C
                                (PC y₂ x₂))
                           · BinProductPr1 C
                               (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂))
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂,
                                 PC y₂ x₂ ⟧,
                           p
                           · BinProductOfArrows C
                               (...) (...) (...) (...)
                           · lens_put C PC h₂ =
                           BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                           · lens_put C PC h₂)
                          (internal_paths_rew_r
                             (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                             (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂)
                              · BinProductOfArrows C
                                  (PC y₂ x₂)
                                  (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                                  (id₁ x₂))
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                                (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))
                             (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂,
                                    PC y₂ x₂ ⟧,
                              p · lens_put C PC h₂ =
                              BinProductOfArrows C ...
                                ... ... ...
                              · lens_put C PC h₂)
                             (idpath
                                (BinProductOfArrows C
                                   ... ... ... ...
                                 · lens_put C PC h₂))
                             (id_left
                                (BinProductOfArrows C
                                   (...) (...) (...)
                                   (...))))
                          (BinProductPr1Commutes C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) x₂
                             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                             (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                             (BinProductPr2 C
                                (PC y₂ x₂))))
                       (assoc
                          (BinProductArrow C
                             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                             (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                             (BinProductPr2 C
                                (PC y₂ x₂))
                           · BinProductPr1 C
                               (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂))
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))
                          (lens_put C PC h₂)))
                    (assoc
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)))
                       (BinProductPr1 C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂))
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂)))
                 (BinProductOfArrowsPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂)
                    (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)))
              (assoc'
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)))
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                    (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                     · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))))
           (id_right
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
               · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x₂ x₂)
                   (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                      (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
                    · lens_put C PC h₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · BinProductPr1 C (PC x₂ x₂))))))

      apply discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat.
  Qed.

C: category

lens_get C PC f · id₁ y · id₁ y =
id₁ x · lens_get C PC f
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC (PC y x) x)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
       (lens_get C PC f) · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
    (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f · id₁ x =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

          apply idpath.
        
C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC (PC y x) x)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
       (lens_get C PC f) · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
    (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f · id₁ x =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x)
· lens_put C PC f

C: category
PC: BinProducts C
x, y: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
is_iso_twosided_disp (pr2 (identity_z_iso x))
  (pr2 (identity_z_iso y))
  (make_lens_mor C PC
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
        (id₁ x · lens_get C PC f) (lens_get C PC f)
        (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧,
         lens_get C PC f · id₁ y · id₁ y = p)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
           (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y)
           (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧, p = lens_get C PC f)
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
              (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y)
              (lens_get C PC f)
              (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧, p = lens_get C PC f)
              (idpath (lens_get C PC f))
              (id_right (lens_get C PC f)))
           (id_right (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y)))
        (id_left (lens_get C PC f))
      :
      lens_get C PC
        (double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp f
           (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id y))
      · identity_z_iso y =
      identity_z_iso x · lens_get C PC f)
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
           (id₁ (PC y x)) (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
             (PC (PC y x) x)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y) (PC y x)
                (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
              · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x)
         · lens_put C PC f · id₁ x)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
           (id₁ (PC y x)) (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
             (PC (PC y x) x)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y) (PC y x)
                (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
              · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x)
         · lens_put C PC f)
        (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
         p =
         BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
              (id₁ (PC y x))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                (PC (PC y x) x)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                   (PC y x) (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
                 · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x)
            · lens_put C PC f)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
              (id₁ (PC y x))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
            · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x)
               · lens_put C PC f))
           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
            p =
            BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
           (internal_paths_rew_r
              (C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧)
              (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
                 (id₁ y) (id₁ x)) (id₁ (PC y x))
              (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧,
               BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (id₁ (PC y x))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
               · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                    (PC (PC y x) x)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                       (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                       (lens_get C PC f)
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                    (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f) =
               p · lens_put C PC f)
              (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                    (id₁ (PC y x))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                  · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                       (PC (PC y x) x)
                       (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                          (lens_get C PC f)
                        · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                       (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f))
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                    (id₁ (PC y x))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                  · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                      (PC (PC y x) x)
                      (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                         (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                         (lens_get C PC f)
                       · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                      (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
                  p = id₁ (PC y x) · lens_put C PC f)
                 (maponpaths_2 compose
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧)
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y x) x)
                          (id₁ (PC y x))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                        · BinProductOfArrows C
                            (PC y x) (PC (PC y x) x)
                            (BinProductOfArrows C
                               (PC y y) (PC y x)
                               (id₁ y)
                               (lens_get C PC f)
                             · BinProductPr1 C
                                 (PC y y)) (id₁ x))
                       (BinProductArrow C (PC y x)
                          (id₁ (PC y x)
                           · (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y y) (PC y x)
                                (id₁ y)
                                (lens_get C PC f)
                              · BinProductPr1 C
                                  (PC y y)))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)
                           · id₁ x))
                       (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧,
                        p =
                        BinProductArrow C (PC y x)
                          (id₁ (PC y x)
                           · BinProductPr1 C (PC y x))
                          (id₁ (PC y x)
                           · BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)))
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y x, y ⟧)
                          (id₁ (PC y x)
                           · (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y y) (PC y x)
                                (id₁ y)
                                (lens_get C PC f)
                              · BinProductPr1 C
                                  (PC y y)))
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y y) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                             (lens_get C PC f)
                           · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                          (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, y ⟧,
                           BinProductArrow C (PC y x)
                             p
                             (BinProductPr2 C (...)
                              · id₁ x) =
                           BinProductArrow C (PC y x)
                             (id₁ (...)
                              · BinProductPr1 C (...))
                             (id₁ (...)
                              · BinProductPr2 C (...)))
                          (internal_paths_rew_r
                             (C ⟦ PC y x, y ⟧)
                             (id₁ (PC y x)
                              · BinProductPr1 C
                                  (PC y x))
                             (BinProductPr1 C (PC y x))
                             (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, y ⟧,
                              BinProductArrow C
                                (PC y x) (... · ...)
                                (... · ...) =
                              BinProductArrow C
                                (PC y x) p (... · ...))
                             (internal_paths_rew_r
                                (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
                                (id₁ (...)
                                 · BinProductPr2 C
                                     (...))
                                (BinProductPr2 C
                                   (PC y x))
                                (λ p : C ⟦ ..., x ⟧,
                                 BinProductArrow C ...
                                   ... ... =
                                 BinProductArrow C ...
                                   ... p)
                                (internal_paths_rew_r
                                   (C ⟦ ..., x ⟧)
                                   (... · ...)
                                   (BinProductPr2 C
                                      ...)
                                   (λ ..., ...)
                                   (internal_paths_rew_r
                                      ... ... ... ...
                                      ... ...)
                                   (id_right ...))
                                (id_left
                                   (BinProductPr2 C
                                      ...)))
                             (id_left
                                (BinProductPr1 C
                                   (PC y x))))
                          (id_left
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y y) (PC y x)
                                (id₁ y)
                                (lens_get C PC f)
                              · BinProductPr1 C
                                  (PC y y))))
                       (postcompWithBinProductArrow C
                          (PC y x) (PC (PC y x) x)
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y y) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                             (lens_get C PC f)
                           · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                          (id₁ x) (id₁ (PC y x))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))) @
                     ! BinProductArrowEta C y x
                         (PC y x) (PC y x)
                         (id₁ (PC y x)))
                    (lens_put C PC f))
                 (assoc
                    (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                       (id₁ (PC y x))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)))
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                       (PC (PC y x) x)
                       (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                          (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                          (lens_get C PC f)
                        · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                       (id₁ x)) (lens_put C PC f)))
              (BinProductOfArrows_id C PC y x))
           (assoc'
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (id₁ (PC y x))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)))
              (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x))
              (lens_put C PC f)))
        (id_right
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
              (id₁ (PC y x))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                (PC (PC y x) x)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                   (PC y x) (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
                 · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x)
            · lens_put C PC f))
      :
      lens_put C PC
        (double_hor_comp lenses_double_cat_hor_comp f
           (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id y))
      · identity_z_iso x =
      BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
        (identity_z_iso y) (identity_z_iso x)
      · lens_put C PC f))

C: category
PC: BinProducts C
double_runitor_laws
  ((λ (x y : C)
    (f : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y),
    make_iso_twosided_disp
      (make_lens_mor C PC
         (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
            (id₁ x · lens_get C PC f)
            (lens_get C PC f)
            (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧,
             lens_get C PC f · id₁ y · id₁ y = p)
            (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
               (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y · id₁ y)
               (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y)
               (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧, p = lens_get C PC f)
               (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
                  (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y)
                  (lens_get C PC f)
                  (λ p : C ⟦ x, y ⟧,
                   p = lens_get C PC f)
                  (idpath (lens_get C PC f))
                  (id_right (lens_get C PC f)))
               (id_right (lens_get C PC f · id₁ y)))
            (id_left (lens_get C PC f))
          :
          lens_get C PC
            (double_hor_comp
               lenses_double_cat_hor_comp f
               (double_id lenses_double_cat_hor_id y))
          · identity_z_iso y =
          identity_z_iso x · lens_get C PC f)
         (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧)
            (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
               (id₁ (PC y x))
               (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
             · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                 (PC (PC y x) x)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y y)
                    (PC y x) (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
                  · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y)) (id₁ x)

               (id₁ (PC y x))
               (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))

             p =
             BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
               (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)

               (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)

                     (PC (PC y x) x)

                        (PC y x) (id₁ y)

                      · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                     (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f))
               (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, x ⟧,
                p =
                BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y x)
                  (id₁ y) (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f)
               (internal_paths_rew_r
                  (C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧)
                  (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                     (PC y x) (id₁ y) (id₁ x))
                  (id₁ (PC y x))
                  (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧,
                   BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y x) x)
                     (id₁ (PC y x))
                     (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x))
                   · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                        (PC (PC y x) x)

                           (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                           (lens_get C PC f)
                         · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                        (id₁ x) · lens_put C PC f) =
                   p · lens_put C PC f)

                              (PC y y) (PC y x)
                              (id₁ y)

                            · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))

                     (BinProductArrow C
                        (PC (PC y x) x) (id₁ (PC y x))

                      · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
                          (PC (PC y x) x)
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y y) (PC y x) (id₁ y)
                             (lens_get C PC f)
                           · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))

                      id₁ (PC y x) · lens_put C PC f)
                     (maponpaths_2 compose
                        (internal_paths_rew_r
                           (C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧)

                              (PC ... x) (id₁ ...)
                              (BinProductPr2 C ...)
                            · BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y x) (PC ... x)
                                (... · ...) (id₁ x))
                           (BinProductArrow C (PC y x)
                              (id₁ ... · (...))
                              (BinProductPr2 C ...
                               · id₁ x))
                           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y x, PC y x ⟧,
                            p =
                            BinProductArrow C (...)
                              (...) (...))
                           (internal_paths_rew_r
                              (C ⟦ PC y x, y ⟧)
                              (id₁ ... · (...))
                              (BinProductOfArrows C
                                 ... ... ... ...
                               · BinProductPr1 C ...)
                              (λ p : ..., ... = ...)
                              (internal_paths_rew_r
                                 (...) (...) (...)
                                 (...) (...) (...))
                              (id_left (...)))
                           (postcompWithBinProductArrow
                              C (PC y x) (PC (...) x)
                              (BinProductOfArrows C
                                 ... ... ... ...
                               · BinProductPr1 C ...)
                              (id₁ x) (id₁ (...))

                             (PC y x) (PC y x)
                             (id₁ (PC y x)))
                        (lens_put C PC f))
                     (assoc

                           (PC (PC y x) x)
                           (id₁ (PC y x))
                           (BinProductPr2 C (PC y x)))

                           (PC (PC y x) x)

                              (PC y y) (PC y x)
                              (id₁ y)

                            · BinProductPr1 C (PC y y))
                           (id₁ x)) (lens_put C PC f)))
                  (BinProductOfArrows_id C PC y x))

                 (id_left (lens_get C PC h₁)))
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                    (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                  · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                      (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                      (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ y₁)
                         (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁)
                         (lens_get C PC h₁)
                       · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₁ y₁))
                      (id₁ x₁) · lens_put C PC h₁
                  · id₁ x₁)
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                    (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                  · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                      (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                      (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ y₁)
                         (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁)
                         (lens_get C PC h₁)
                       · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₁ y₁))
                      (id₁ x₁) · lens_put C PC h₁)
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧,
                  p =
                  BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                    (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                  · lens_put C PC h₁)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)

                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                     · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                         (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                         (BinProductOfArrows C

                            (id₁ y₁)
                            (lens_get C PC h₁)
                          · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₁ y₁))
                         (id₁ x₁) · lens_put C PC h₁)
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                       (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₁ x₁)
                          (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                          (BinProductOfArrows C

                             (id₁ y₁)
                             (lens_get C PC h₁)
                           · BinProductPr1 C
                               (PC y₁ y₁)) (id₁ x₁)
                        · lens_put C PC h₁))
                    (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧,
                     p =
                     BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₁ x₁)
                       (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁)
                     · lens_put C PC h₁)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, PC y₁ x₁ ⟧)
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₁ x₁) (PC y₁ x₁)
                          (id₁ y₁) (id₁ x₁))
                       (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                       (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, PC y₁ x₁ ⟧,
                        BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                          (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁))

                              · BinProductPr1 C
                                  (PC y₁ y₁)) (id₁ x₁)
                           · lens_put C PC h₁) =
                        p · lens_put C PC h₁)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧)
                          (BinProductArrow C
                             (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                             (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                             (BinProductPr2 C
                                (PC y₁ x₁))
                           · (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC y₁ x₁)
                                (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)

                                (id₁ x₁)
                              · lens_put C PC h₁))
                          (BinProductArrow C

                             (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                             (BinProductPr2 C
                                (PC y₁ x₁))
                           · BinProductOfArrows C
                               (PC y₁ x₁)
                               (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                               (BinProductOfArrows C
                                  (PC y₁ y₁)
                                  (PC y₁ x₁) (id₁ y₁)
                                  (lens_get C PC h₁)
                                · BinProductPr1 C
                                    (PC y₁ y₁))
                               (id₁ x₁)
                           · lens_put C PC h₁)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧,
                           p =
                           id₁ (PC y₁ x₁)
                           · lens_put C PC h₁)
                          (maponpaths_2 compose
                             (internal_paths_rew_r
                                (C ⟦ PC y₁ x₁,
                                 PC y₁ x₁ ⟧)

                                      ...)

                                      ... · id₁ x₁))

                                       PC y₁ x₁ ⟧,
                                 p =
                                 BinProductArrow C
                                   (...) (...) (...))
                                (internal_paths_rew_r

                                   (id₁ ... · (...))
                                   (BinProductOfArrows
                                      C ... ... ...
                                      ...

                                        ...)

                                    ... = ...)

                                      (...) (...)
                                      (...) (...)
                                      (...) (...))

                                      C ... ... ...
                                      ...
                                    · BinProductPr1 C
                                        ...) (id₁ x₁)
                                   (id₁ (...))
                                   (BinProductPr2 C
                                      (...))) @
                              ! BinProductArrowEta C

                                  (PC y₁ x₁)
                                  (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁)))

                          (assoc
                             (BinProductArrow C
                                (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)
                                (id₁ (PC y₁ x₁))
                                (BinProductPr2 C
                                   (PC y₁ x₁)))

                                (id₁ x₁))
                             (lens_put C PC h₁)))
                       (BinProductOfArrows_id C PC y₁
                          x₁))
                    (assoc'
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₁ x₁) x₁)

                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₁ x₁)))

                          · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₁ y₁))
                         (id₁ x₁) · lens_put C PC h₁))))) ;;2 τ) =
double_hor_comp_mor lenses_double_cat_hor_comp τ
  (double_id_mor lenses_double_cat_hor_id v₂) ;;2 
make_iso_twosided_disp
  (make_lens_mor C PC
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
        (id₁ x₂ · lens_get C PC h₂) (lens_get C PC h₂)
        (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧,
         lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂ · id₁ y₂ = p)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
           (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂ · id₁ y₂)
           (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)
           (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧, p = lens_get C PC h₂)
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
              (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)
              (lens_get C PC h₂)
              (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧,
               p = lens_get C PC h₂)
              (idpath (lens_get C PC h₂))
              (id_right (lens_get C PC h₂)))
           (id_right (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)))
        (id_left (lens_get C PC h₂)))
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
           (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))

         · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (lens_get C PC h₂)
              · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂)) (id₁ x₂)
         · lens_put C PC h₂ · id₁ x₂)
        (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
           (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))

         · lens_put C PC h₂)
        (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
         p =
         BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
           (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)

            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)

           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
            p =

              (internal_paths_rew_r

              (BinProductOfArrows_id C PC y₂ x₂))
