           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
              (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂ · id₁ y₂)
              (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)
              (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧,
               p = lens_get C PC h₂)
              (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
                 (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)
                 (lens_get C PC h₂)
                 (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧,
                  p = lens_get C PC h₂)
                 (idpath (lens_get C PC h₂))
                 (id_right (lens_get C PC h₂)))
              (id_right (lens_get C PC h₂ · id₁ y₂)))
           (id_left (lens_get C PC h₂)))
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                   (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                   (lens_get C PC h₂)
                 · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂ · id₁ x₂)
           (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
              (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
              (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                   (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                   (lens_get C PC h₂)
                 · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
           (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
            p =
            BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
              (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
               · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                   (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                      (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                      (lens_get C PC h₂)
                    · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                   (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
               · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                       (lens_get C PC h₂)
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                    (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂))
              (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
               p =
               BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                 (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂)
               · lens_put C PC h₂)
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂) (id₁ x₂))
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧,
                  BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                  · (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ y₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (id₁ y₂) (lens_get C PC h₂)
                        · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                       (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂) =
                  p · lens_put C PC h₂)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                     · (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ y₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂)
                             (lens_get C PC h₂)
                           · BinProductPr1 C
                               (PC y₂ y₂)) (id₁ x₂)
                        · lens_put C PC h₂))
                    (BinProductArrow C
                       (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                       (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                       (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
                     · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                         (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                         (BinProductOfArrows C
                            (PC y₂ y₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                            (id₁ y₂)
                            (lens_get C PC h₂)
                          · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                         (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
                    (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                     p =
                     id₁ (PC y₂ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)
                    (maponpaths_2 compose
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, PC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                          (BinProductArrow C
                             (PC (...) x₂) (id₁ (...))
                             (BinProductPr2 C (...))
                           · BinProductOfArrows C
                               (PC y₂ x₂)
                               (PC (...) x₂)
                               (BinProductOfArrows C
                                  ... ... ... ...
                                · BinProductPr1 C ...)
                               (id₁ x₂))
                          (BinProductArrow C
                             (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ (...) · (... · ...))
                             (BinProductPr2 C (...)
                              · id₁ x₂))
                          (λ p : C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂,
                                 PC y₂ x₂ ⟧,
                           p =
                           BinProductArrow C
                             (PC y₂ x₂) (... · ...)
                             (... · ...))
                          (internal_paths_rew_r
                             (C ⟦ PC y₂ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
                             (id₁ (...) · (... · ...))
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (...) (...) (...)
                                (...)
                              · BinProductPr1 C (...))
                             (λ p : C ⟦ ..., y₂ ⟧,
                              BinProductArrow C ... p
                                ... =
                              BinProductArrow C ...
                                ... ...)
                             (internal_paths_rew_r
                                (C ⟦ ..., y₂ ⟧)
                                (... · ...)
                                (BinProductPr1 C ...)
                                (λ ..., ...)
                                (internal_paths_rew_r
                                   ... ... ... ... ...
                                   ...) (id_left ...))
                             (id_left (... · ...)))
                          (postcompWithBinProductArrow
                             C (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                             (BinProductOfArrows C
                                (...) (...) (...)
                                (...)
                              · BinProductPr1 C (...))
                             (id₁ x₂) (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                             (BinProductPr2 C
                                (PC y₂ x₂))) @
                        ! BinProductArrowEta C y₂ x₂
                            (PC y₂ x₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                            (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂)))
                       (lens_put C PC h₂))
                    (assoc
                       (BinProductArrow C
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                          (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)))
                       (BinProductOfArrows C
                          (PC y₂ x₂)
                          (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                          (BinProductOfArrows C
                             (PC y₂ y₂) (PC y₂ x₂)
                             (id₁ y₂)
                             (lens_get C PC h₂)
                           · BinProductPr1 C
                               (PC y₂ y₂)) (id₁ x₂))
                       (lens_put C PC h₂)))
                 (BinProductOfArrows_id C PC y₂ x₂))
              (assoc'
                 (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂)))
                 (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                    (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                       (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                       (lens_get C PC h₂)
                     · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                    (id₁ x₂)) (lens_put C PC h₂)))
           (id_right
              (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                 (id₁ (PC y₂ x₂))
                 (BinProductPr2 C (PC y₂ x₂))
               · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ x₂)
                   (PC (PC y₂ x₂) x₂)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y₂ y₂)
                      (PC y₂ x₂) (id₁ y₂)
                      (lens_get C PC h₂)
                    · BinProductPr1 C (PC y₂ y₂))
                   (id₁ x₂) · lens_put C PC h₂)))))

      apply discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat.
  Qed.

C: category
PC: BinProducts C
w, x, y, z: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC w x
g: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
h: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z
BinProductArrow C (PC (PC z w) w) (id₁ (PC z w))
  (BinProductPr2 C (PC z w))
· BinProductOfArrows C (PC x w) (PC (PC z w) w)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (PC z x) (PC z w) (id₁ z)
       (lens_get C PC f)
     · (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC z x) x)
          (id₁ (PC z x)) (BinProductPr2 C (PC z x))
        · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x)
            (PC (PC z x) x)
            (BinProductOfArrows C (PC z y) (PC z x)
               (id₁ z) (lens_get C PC g)
             · lens_put C PC h) (id₁ x)
        · lens_put C PC g)) (id₁ w) · lens_put C PC f
· id₁ w =
BinProductOfArrows C (PC z w) (PC z w) (id₁ z) (id₁ w)
· (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC z w) w) (id₁ (PC z w))
     (BinProductPr2 C (PC z w))
   · BinProductOfArrows C (PC y w) (PC (PC z w) w)
       (BinProductOfArrows C (PC z y) (PC z w) (id₁ z)
          (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g)
        · lens_put C PC h) (id₁ w)
   · (BinProductArrow C (PC (PC y w) w) (id₁ (PC y w))
        (BinProductPr2 C (PC y w))
      · BinProductOfArrows C (PC x w) (PC (PC y w) w)
          (BinProductOfArrows C (PC y x) (PC y w)
             (id₁ y) (lens_get C PC f)
           · lens_put C PC g) (id₁ w)
      · lens_put C PC f))

C: category
PC: BinProducts C
w, x, y, z: C
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC w x
g: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y
h: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z
is_iso_twosided_disp (pr2 (identity_z_iso w))
  (pr2 (identity_z_iso z))
  (make_lens_mor C PC
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ w, z ⟧)
        (id₁ w
         · (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
            · lens_get C PC h))
        (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
         · lens_get C PC h)
        (λ p : C ⟦ w, z ⟧,
         lens_get C PC f
         · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h) · id₁ z =
         p)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ w, z ⟧)
           (lens_get C PC f
            · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h)
            · id₁ z)
           (lens_get C PC f
            · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h))
           (λ p : C ⟦ w, z ⟧,
            p =
            lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
            · lens_get C PC h)
           (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ w, z ⟧)
              (lens_get C PC f
               · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h))
              (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
               · lens_get C PC h)
              (λ p : C ⟦ w, z ⟧,
               p =
               lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
               · lens_get C PC h)
              (idpath
                 (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g

C: category
PC: BinProducts C
double_associator_laws
  ((λ (w x y z : C)
    (f : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC w x)
    (g : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC x y)
    (h : twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses C PC y z),
    make_iso_twosided_disp
      (make_lens_mor C PC
         (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ w, z ⟧)
            (id₁ w
             · (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
                · lens_get C PC h))
            (lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
             · lens_get C PC h)
            (λ p : C ⟦ w, z ⟧,
             lens_get C PC f
             · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h)
             · id₁ z = p)
            (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ w, z ⟧)
               (lens_get C PC f
                · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h)
                · id₁ z)
               (lens_get C PC f
                · (lens_get C PC g · lens_get C PC h))
               (λ p : C ⟦ w, z ⟧,
                p =
                lens_get C PC f · lens_get C PC g
                · lens_get C PC h)
               (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ w, z ⟧)
                  (lens_get C PC f
                   · (lens_get C PC g
                      · lens_get C PC h))

                                       (PC (PC z₂ w₂)
                                          w₂)
                                       (BinProductOfArrows
                                          C (PC z₂ y₂)
                                          (PC z₂ w₂)
                                          (id₁ z₂)
                                          (lens_get C
                                             PC h₂
                                           · lens_get
                                               C PC j₂)
                                        · lens_put C
                                            PC k₂)
                                       (id₁ w₂))
                                    (BinProductArrow C
                                       (PC (PC y₂ w₂)
                                          w₂)
                                       (id₁ (PC y₂ w₂))
                                       (BinProductPr2
                                          C (PC y₂ w₂))
                                     · BinProductOfArrows
                                         C (PC x₂ w₂)
                                         (PC
                                            (PC y₂ w₂)
                                            w₂)
                                         (BinProductOfArrows
                                            C
                                            (PC y₂ x₂)
                                            (PC y₂ w₂)
                                            (id₁ y₂)
                                            (lens_get
                                               C PC h₂)
                                          · lens_put C
                                              PC j₂)
                                         (id₁ w₂)
                                     · lens_put C PC
                                         h₂)))
                              (assoc'
                                 (BinProductArrow C
                                    (PC (PC z₂ x₂) x₂)
                                    (id₁ (PC z₂ x₂))
                                    (BinProductPr2 C
                                       (PC z₂ x₂)))
                                 (BinProductOfArrows C
                                    (PC y₂ x₂)
                                    (PC (PC z₂ x₂) x₂)
                                    (BinProductOfArrows
                                       C (PC z₂ y₂)
                                       (PC z₂ x₂)
                                       (id₁ z₂)
                                       (lens_get C PC
                                          j₂)
                                     · lens_put C PC
                                         k₂) (id₁ x₂))
                                 (lens_put C PC j₂)))
                           (assoc'
                              (BinProductArrow C
                                 (PC (PC z₂ w₂) w₂)
                                 (id₁ (PC z₂ w₂))
                                 (BinProductPr2 C
                                    (PC z₂ w₂)))
                              (BinProductOfArrows C
                                 (PC x₂ w₂)
                                 (PC (PC z₂ w₂) w₂)
                                 (BinProductOfArrows C
                                    (PC z₂ x₂)
                                    (PC z₂ w₂)
                                    (id₁ z₂)
                                    (lens_get C PC h₂)
                                  · (BinProductArrow C
                                       (PC (PC z₂ x₂)
                                          x₂)
                                       (id₁ (PC z₂ x₂))
                                       (BinProductPr2
                                          C (PC z₂ x₂))
                                     · BinProductOfArrows
                                         C (PC y₂ x₂)
                                         (PC
                                            (PC z₂ x₂)
                                            x₂)
                                         (BinProductOfArrows
                                            C
                                            (PC z₂ y₂)
                                            (PC z₂ x₂)
                                            (id₁ z₂)
                                            (lens_get
                                               C PC j₂)
                                          · lens_put C
                                              PC k₂)
                                         (id₁ x₂)
                                     · lens_put C PC
                                         j₂)) (id₁ w₂))
                              (lens_put C PC h₂)))
                        (id_right
                           (BinProductArrow C
                              (PC (PC z₂ w₂) w₂)
                              (id₁ (PC z₂ w₂))
                              (BinProductPr2 C
                                 (PC z₂ w₂))
                            · BinProductOfArrows C
                                (PC x₂ w₂)
                                (PC (PC z₂ w₂) w₂)
                                (BinProductOfArrows C
                                   (PC z₂ x₂)
                                   (PC z₂ w₂) (id₁ z₂)
                                   (lens_get C PC h₂)
                                 · (BinProductArrow C
                                      (PC (PC z₂ x₂)
                                         x₂)
                                      (id₁ (PC z₂ x₂))
                                      (BinProductPr2 C
                                         (PC z₂ x₂))
                                    · BinProductOfArrows
                                        C (PC y₂ x₂)
                                        (PC (PC z₂ x₂)
                                           x₂)
                                        (BinProductOfArrows
                                           C
                                           (PC z₂ y₂)
                                           (PC z₂ x₂)
                                           (id₁ z₂)
                                           (lens_get C
                                              PC j₂)
                                         · lens_put C
                                             PC k₂)
                                        (id₁ x₂)
                                    · lens_put C PC j₂))
                                (id₁ w₂)
                            · lens_put C PC h₂)))))

      apply discrete_lenses_twosided_disp_cat.
  Qed.
End LensesDoubleCat.
